Ironic, seeing how they made rock-and-roll-esque songs and toured with rock-and-roll-loving band <a href="/wiki/The_Clash" title="The Clash">The Clash</a>. Believe it or not, some years later, <a href="/wiki/Is_Vic_There%3F" title="Is Vic There?">a song</a> was made dedicated to the lead singer <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vic_Goddard" title="Vic Goddard">Vic Goddard</a>, who had by then quit to become a postman.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><b><a href="/wiki/Thai_Elephant_Orchestra" title="Thai Elephant Orchestra">Thai Elephant Orchestra</a></b>
</td>
<td>An orchestra of elephants playing specially-designed instruments.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><b><a href="/wiki/Tout-%C3%A0-Coup_Jazz" title="Tout-à-Coup Jazz">Tout-à-Coup Jazz</a></b>
</td>
<td>An African <a href="/wiki/Jazz" title="Jazz">jazz</a> band from the 1970s whose membership included two future <a href="/wiki/Burkina_Faso" title="Burkina Faso">Burkinabé</a> leaders, <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Sankara" title="Thomas Sankara">Thomas Sankara</a> and <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Compaor%C3%A9" title="Blaise Compaoré">Blaise Compaoré</a>, with the latter overthrowing the other in a 1987 coup. Unbelievably, the band's name was purely coincidental.
</td></tr>

</td>
<td>TV signals in <a href="/wiki/Chicago" title="Chicago">Chicago</a> are twice overpowered on 22 November 1987 by broadcasts featuring a person (possibly a male) disguised as the 1980s virtual TV character <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Max_Headroom_(character)" title="Max Headroom (character)">Max Headroom</a>. The source of the broadcasts and the people involved remain unknown. Ten years previously, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Southern_Television_broadcast_interruption_hoax" title="Southern Television broadcast interruption hoax">the sound during a broadcast by the UK's Southern Television is replaced</a> by a voice claiming to be an extraterrestrial named "Vrillon".

<td>The philosophical or scientific argument that tries to appear <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Skeptical" title="Skeptical">skeptical</a>, but really is trying to prove a position, as in "<a href="/wiki/Moon_landing_conspiracy_theories" title="Moon landing conspiracy theories">I don’t see enough evidence that we landed on the moon</a>".
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><b><a href="/wiki/Saeculum_obscurum" title="Saeculum obscurum">Pornocracy</a></b>
</td>
<td>The period of the papacy in the early 10th century, beginning with <a href="/wiki/Pope_Sergius_III" title="Pope Sergius III">Pope Sergius III</a> from 904 and ending with the death of <a href="/wiki/Pope_John_XII" title="Pope John XII">Pope John XII</a> in 963. During this period, the popes were under the influence of corrupt women (though not necessarily <a href="/wiki/Prostitution" title="Prostitution">prostitutes</a>), especially <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Theodora_(10th_century)" title="Theodora (10th century)">Theodora</a> and her daughter, <a href="/wiki/Marozia" title="Marozia">Marozia</a>. This period is also called <i>Saeculum obscurum</i> or the "Rule of the Harlots".
</td></tr>
